1d:T4be54,<h2
id="javascript高级程序设计红宝书第二遍阅读动手实践">《JavaScript高级程序设计》红宝书第二遍阅读（动手实践）</h2>
<h3 id="第1章什么是javascript">第1章——什么是JavaScript</h3>
<p>DOM将整个页面抽象为一组分层节点。</p>
<p>BOM用于支持访问和操作浏览器的窗口。</p>
<hr />
<h3 id="第2章html中的javascript">第2章——HTML中的JavaScript</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>2.1 &lt; script &gt;元素</strong></li>
</ul>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>元素</th>
<th>描述</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>async</td>
<td>立即开始下载脚本，但不能阻止其他页面动作，比如下载资源或等待其他脚本加载，只对外部脚本文件有效；</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>charset</td>
<td>使用src指定代码字符集，很少使用，大多数浏览器不在乎它的值；</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>crossorigin</td>
<td>配置相关CORS(跨源资源共享)设置。默认不使用CORS；</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>defer</td>
<td>表示在文档解析和显示完成后，再执行脚本，只对外部脚本文件有效；</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>integrity</td>
<td>运行比对接收到的资源和指定的加密签名以验证子资源的完整性(SRI，Subresource
Intergrity)。可以用于确保内容分发网络（CDN，Content Delivery
Network）不会提供恶意内容。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>src</td>
<td>包含要执行的代码的外部文件；</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>type</td>
<td>表示代码中脚本语言的内容类型（也称MIMI类型），这个值始终是“text/javascript”，如果这个值是module，则代码会被当作ES6模块，而且只有这种时候，代码中才能出现import和export关键字。</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>2.1.3 异步加载脚本</strong></p>
<p>async属性和defer，两者都能适用于外部脚本，告诉浏览器立即开始下载。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb1"><pre
class="sourceCode html"><code class="sourceCode html"><span id="cb1-1"><a href="#cb1-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="dt">&lt;</span><span class="kw">html</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-2"><a href="#cb1-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">&lt;</span><span class="kw">head</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-3"><a href="#cb1-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">&lt;</span><span class="kw">title</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span>异步执行脚本<span class="dt">&lt;/</span><span class="kw">title</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-4"><a href="#cb1-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">&lt;</span><span class="kw">script</span><span class="ot"> async src</span><span class="op">=</span><span class="st">&quot;main.js&gt;</span><span class="er">&lt;</span><span class="st">/script&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-5"><a href="#cb1-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="st">    </span><span class="er">&lt;</span><span class="st">script async src=&quot;</span><span class="ot">main1.js</span><span class="dt">&gt;&lt;/</span><span class="kw">script</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span><span class="co">&lt;!--可能先于第一个脚本执行--&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-6"><a href="#cb1-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">&lt;/</span><span class="kw">head</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-7"><a href="#cb1-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">&lt;</span><span class="kw">body</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-8"><a href="#cb1-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">&lt;/</span><span class="kw">body</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb1-9"><a href="#cb1-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="dt">&lt;/</span><span class="kw">html</span><span class="dt">&gt;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>2.1.4 动态加载脚本</strong></p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb2"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb2-1"><a href="#cb2-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> script <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">document</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">createElement</span>(<span class="st">&#39;script&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-2"><a href="#cb2-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>script<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">src</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;gibberish.js&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-3"><a href="#cb2-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>script<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">async</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">false</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb2-4"><a href="#cb2-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">document</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">head</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">appendChild</span>(script)<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<hr />
<h3 id="第3章语言基础">第3章——语言基础</h3>
<p>var声明的变量会被提升（hoist），把所有变量声明都拿到函数作用域顶部，在函数退出时被销毁。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb3"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb3-1"><a href="#cb3-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//var 提升（hoist）</span></span>
<span id="cb3-2"><a href="#cb3-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">foo</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb3-3"><a href="#cb3-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(age)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-4"><a href="#cb3-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">var</span> age <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">21</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-5"><a href="#cb3-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb3-6"><a href="#cb3-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">foo</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-7"><a href="#cb3-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// ↑上面的相当于提升后的下面↓</span></span>
<span id="cb3-8"><a href="#cb3-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">foo</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb3-9"><a href="#cb3-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">var</span> age<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//把所有变量声明都拿到函数作用域顶部</span></span>
<span id="cb3-10"><a href="#cb3-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(age)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-11"><a href="#cb3-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    age <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">21</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb3-12"><a href="#cb3-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb3-13"><a href="#cb3-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">foo</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>let声明的范围是<strong>块作用域</strong>，var声明的范围是<strong>函数作用域</strong>。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb4"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb4-1"><a href="#cb4-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//let声明</span></span>
<span id="cb4-2"><a href="#cb4-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">f1</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb4-3"><a href="#cb4-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">let</span> n <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">5</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb4-4"><a href="#cb4-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="cf">if</span>(<span class="kw">true</span>){</span>
<span id="cb4-5"><a href="#cb4-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">let</span> n <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb4-6"><a href="#cb4-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb4-7"><a href="#cb4-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(n)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// 5 使用let声明的变量 外层代码块 不受 内层代码块 的影响。</span></span>
<span id="cb4-8"><a href="#cb4-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//var声明</span></span>
<span id="cb4-9"><a href="#cb4-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">f1</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb4-10"><a href="#cb4-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="kw">var</span> n <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">5</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb4-11"><a href="#cb4-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="cf">if</span>(<span class="kw">true</span>){</span>
<span id="cb4-12"><a href="#cb4-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">var</span> n <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb4-13"><a href="#cb4-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  }</span>
<span id="cb4-14"><a href="#cb4-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(n)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// 10 使用var定义变量n，块作用域下最后输出的值是 内层代码块 的结果。</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>const声明范围也是<strong>块作用域</strong>，是必须同时<strong>初始化变量</strong>。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb5"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb5-1"><a href="#cb5-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> age <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;kuishou&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-2"><a href="#cb5-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">if</span>(<span class="kw">true</span>){</span>
<span id="cb5-3"><a href="#cb5-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">const</span> name <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;zhangsan&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb5-4"><a href="#cb5-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb5-5"><a href="#cb5-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(age)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//kuisou </span></span>
<span id="cb5-6"><a href="#cb5-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(name)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//undefined 块作用域只能拿到当前层代码块的结果。</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>注意</strong>：平时使用中，const优先，let次之。</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>3.4数据类型</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>typeof操作符：用来区分函数和其他对象</p>
<p><strong>undefined 和 null 的****区别</strong>：</p>
<p><strong>undefined
类型</strong>：表示声明了变量但是未初始化（没有值），undefined是由null中派生而来的。</p>
<p><strong>null类型</strong>：表示一个空对象指针。</p>
<p><strong>boolean类型</strong>：要将一个其他类型的值转换成布尔值，可以调用Boolean()转换函数。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb6"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb6-1"><a href="#cb6-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> message <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;Hello kuishou&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb6-2"><a href="#cb6-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">if</span>(message){</span>
<span id="cb6-3"><a href="#cb6-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;message 已经转换成布尔类型&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb6-4"><a href="#cb6-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="co">//if等流控制语句会自动执行其他类型转换为布尔类型语句</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>Number类型</strong>：表示整数和浮点值，范围在Number.MIN_VALUE~Number.MAX_VALUE之间。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb7"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb7-1"><a href="#cb7-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> <span class="bu">Number</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">68</span><span class="op">;</span>    <span class="co">//整数</span></span>
<span id="cb7-2"><a href="#cb7-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb7-3"><a href="#cb7-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> octalNum1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bn">070</span><span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//八进制56</span></span>
<span id="cb7-4"><a href="#cb7-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> octalNum3 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">08</span><span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//无效的八进制数，当成8处理</span></span>
<span id="cb7-5"><a href="#cb7-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb7-6"><a href="#cb7-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> folatNum1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bn">0xA</span><span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//十六进制10</span></span>
<span id="cb7-7"><a href="#cb7-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> folatNum2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bn">0x1f</span><span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//十六进制31</span></span>
<span id="cb7-8"><a href="#cb7-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb7-9"><a href="#cb7-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> floatNum1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fl">1.1</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb7-10"><a href="#cb7-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> floatNum2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fl">0.1</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb7-11"><a href="#cb7-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> floatNum3 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="op">.</span><span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//有效，但不推荐</span></span>
<span id="cb7-12"><a href="#cb7-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb7-13"><a href="#cb7-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> floatNum4 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fl">1.</span> <span class="co">//小数点后面没有数字，当做1处理</span></span>
<span id="cb7-14"><a href="#cb7-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> floatNum5 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fl">10.0</span> <span class="co">//小数点后面是0，当成整数处理</span></span>
<span id="cb7-15"><a href="#cb7-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb7-16"><a href="#cb7-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> floatNum6 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fl">3.153e7</span><span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//以3.153为系数，乘以10的7次幂；</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>NaN</strong>（Not a
Number）：意思'不是数值',<strong>表示</strong>本来要返回数值的操作失败了。</p>
<p><strong>isNaN()
函数</strong>：接收一个任意类型的参数，判断这个参数是否‘不是数值’</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb8"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb8-1"><a href="#cb8-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="pp">isNaN</span>(<span class="kw">NaN</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//true</span></span>
<span id="cb8-2"><a href="#cb8-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="pp">isNaN</span>(<span class="dv">10</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//false,10是数值</span></span>
<span id="cb8-3"><a href="#cb8-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="pp">isNaN</span>(<span class="st">&quot;10&quot;</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//false,可以转换为数组</span></span>
<span id="cb8-4"><a href="#cb8-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="pp">isNaN</span>(<span class="st">&quot;blue&quot;</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//true,不可以转换为数值</span></span>
<span id="cb8-5"><a href="#cb8-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="pp">isNaN</span>(<span class="kw">true</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//false,可以转换成数值1</span></span>
<span id="cb8-6"><a href="#cb8-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb8-7"><a href="#cb8-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Number</span>(<span class="st">&quot;Hello kuishou&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//NaN  字符串&quot;Hello kushou&quot;找不到对应的值的时候会提示NaN</span></span>
<span id="cb8-8"><a href="#cb8-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Number</span>(<span class="st">&quot;&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span>             <span class="co">//0</span></span>
<span id="cb8-9"><a href="#cb8-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num3 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Number</span>(<span class="st">&quot;000011&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span>       <span class="co">//11</span></span>
<span id="cb8-10"><a href="#cb8-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num4 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Number</span>(<span class="kw">true</span>)<span class="op">;</span>           <span class="co">//1</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>数值转换</strong>：Number、parseInt()、parseFloat()</p>
<p><strong>paresInt()
函数</strong>：能识别不同的整数格式（十进制、八进制、十六进制）</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb9"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb9-1"><a href="#cb9-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;1234blue&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//1234</span></span>
<span id="cb9-2"><a href="#cb9-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span>        <span class="co">//NaN</span></span>
<span id="cb9-3"><a href="#cb9-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num3 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;0xA&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span>     <span class="co">//10,解释为十六进制</span></span>
<span id="cb9-4"><a href="#cb9-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num4 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="fl">22.5</span>)<span class="op">;</span>      <span class="co">//22</span></span>
<span id="cb9-5"><a href="#cb9-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num5 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;70&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span>      <span class="co">//70,解释为十进制</span></span>
<span id="cb9-6"><a href="#cb9-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb9-7"><a href="#cb9-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;10&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">2</span>)<span class="op">;</span>    <span class="co">//2,按二进制解析</span></span>
<span id="cb9-8"><a href="#cb9-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;10&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">8</span>)<span class="op">;</span>    <span class="co">//8,按十进制解析</span></span>
<span id="cb9-9"><a href="#cb9-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num3 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;10&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">10</span>)<span class="op">;</span>   <span class="co">//10,按十进制解析</span></span>
<span id="cb9-10"><a href="#cb9-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num4 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="pp">parseInt</span>(<span class="st">&quot;10&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">16</span>)<span class="op">;</span>   <span class="co">//16，按十六进制解析</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>String
类型</strong>：可以用双引号（"）、单引号（'）、反引号（`）标示。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb10"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb10-1"><a href="#cb10-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> Name <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;kuishou&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb10-2"><a href="#cb10-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> Name <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;lingxiu&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb10-3"><a href="#cb10-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> Name <span class="op">=</span> <span class="vs">`jianlin`</span><span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>toSting()</strong>： 转换为字符串。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb11"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb11-1"><a href="#cb11-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb11-2"><a href="#cb11-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(num<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">toString</span>(<span class="dv">2</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//1010,转换成二进制数</span></span>
<span id="cb11-3"><a href="#cb11-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb11-4"><a href="#cb11-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;kuishou&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb11-5"><a href="#cb11-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">String</span>(num))<span class="op">;</span>   <span class="co">//kuishou</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>模板字面量</strong>：求值后得到的字符串，保留换行字符，可以跨行定义字符串。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb12"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb12-1"><a href="#cb12-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> myMultLineString <span class="op">=</span> <span class="vs">`first line</span><span class="sc">\n</span><span class="vs">second line`</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb12-2"><a href="#cb12-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> myMultLineTemplatLiteral <span class="op">=</span> <span class="vs">`first line second line`</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb12-3"><a href="#cb12-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(myMultLineString)<span class="op">;</span>                              <span class="co">//first line</span></span>
<span id="cb12-4"><a href="#cb12-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                                                            <span class="co">// second line</span></span>
<span id="cb12-5"><a href="#cb12-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(myMultLineTemplatLiteral)<span class="op">;</span>                      <span class="co">//first line second line</span></span>
<span id="cb12-6"><a href="#cb12-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="fu">log</span>(myMultLineString <span class="op">==</span> myMultLineTemplatLiteral)<span class="op">;</span>  <span class="co">//true</span></span>
<span id="cb12-7"><a href="#cb12-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//模板字面量在定义模板时特别有用，比如下面这个 HTML 模板:</span></span>
<span id="cb12-8"><a href="#cb12-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> <span class="vs">`</span></span>
<span id="cb12-9"><a href="#cb12-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="vs">&lt;div&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb12-10"><a href="#cb12-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="vs">    &lt;a href=&quot;#&quot;&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb12-11"><a href="#cb12-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="vs">        &lt;span&gt;kuishou&lt;/span&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb12-12"><a href="#cb12-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="vs">    &lt;/a&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb12-13"><a href="#cb12-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="vs">&lt;/div&gt;</span></span>
<span id="cb12-14"><a href="#cb12-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="vs">`</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>字符串插值</strong>：可以在一个连续定义中插入一个或多个值。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb13"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb13-1"><a href="#cb13-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> value <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">5</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb13-2"><a href="#cb13-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> exponent <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;second&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>

<p><strong>Symbol类型</strong>：确保<strong>对象属性</strong>使用使用唯一的标识符，不会发生冲突的危险。是用来创建唯一记号，进而用作非
字符串形式的对象属性。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb15"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb15-1"><a href="#cb15-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> o <span class="op">=</span> {</span>
<span id="cb15-2"><a href="#cb15-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    [<span class="bu">Symbol</span>(<span class="st">&#39;fool&#39;</span>)]<span class="op">:</span><span class="st">&#39;foo val&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span> </span>
<span id="cb15-3"><a href="#cb15-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    [<span class="bu">Symbol</span>(<span class="st">&#39;bar&#39;</span>)]<span class="op">:</span><span class="st">&#39;bar val&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb15-4"><a href="#cb15-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb15-5"><a href="#cb15-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(o)<span class="op">;</span>             <span class="co">//{Symbol(fool): &quot;foo val&quot;, Symbol(bar): &quot;bar val&quot;}</span></span>
<span id="cb15-6"><a href="#cb15-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb15-7"><a href="#cb15-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> barSymbol <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Object</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">getOwnPropertySymbols</span>(o)</span>
<span id="cb15-8"><a href="#cb15-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                <span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">find</span>((symbol) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> symbol<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">toString</span>()<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">match</span>(<span class="ss">/bar/</span>))<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb15-9"><a href="#cb15-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(barSymbol)<span class="op">;</span>     <span class="co">//Symbol(bar)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Symbol符号</th>
<th>属性</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.asyncItertor</td>
<td>一个方法，该方法返回的对象默认到的AsyncItertor,由for-await-of语句使用。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.hasInstance</td>
<td>一个方法，该方法决定一个构造器对象是否认可的一个对象是它的实例。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.isConcatSpreadable</td>
<td>一个布尔值，如果是true,则意味着对象应该用Array.protype.concat()打平其数组元素。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.iterator</td>
<td>一个方法，该方法返回<strong>对象默认的迭代器</strong>，由for-of语句使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.match</td>
<td>一个正则表达式，该方法用<strong>正则表达式</strong>去匹配字符串。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.replace</td>
<td>一个正则表达式方法，该方法<strong>替换</strong>一个字符串中匹配的字符</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.search</td>
<td>一个正则表达式方法，该方法返回字符串中匹配<strong>正则表达式的索引</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.species</td>
<td>一个函数值，该函数作为创建<strong>派生对象</strong>的构造函数</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.spilt</td>
<td>一个正则表达式方法，该方法在匹配正则表达式的索引位置拆分字符串。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.toPrimitve</td>
<td>一个方法，该方法将对象转换为相应的原始值。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.toStringTag</td>
<td>一个字符串，该字符串用于创建对象的默认字符串描述。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symbol.unscopables</td>
<td>一个对象，该对象所有的以及继承的属性，都会从关联对象的With环境绑定中排除。</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><strong>Object 类型</strong>：通过创建 Object
类型的实例来创建自己的对象，然后再给对象添加属性和方法。</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Object实例</th>
<th>属性</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>constructor</td>
<td>用于创建当前对象的函数。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>hasOwnProperty(propertyName)</td>
<td>用于判断当前对象实例（不是原型）上是否存在给定的属性。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>isPrototypeOf(object)</td>
<td>用于判断当前对象是否为另一个对象的原型。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>propertyIsEnumerable(propertyName)</td>
<td>用于判断给定的属性是否可以使用。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>toLocaleString()</td>
<td>返回对象的字符串表示，该字符串反映对象所在的本地化执行环境。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>toString()</td>
<td>返回对象的字符串表示。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>valueOf()</td>
<td>返回对象对应的字符串、数值或布尔值表示。</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<ul>
<li><strong>3.5一元操作符（只操作一个值的操作符）</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>位操作符：有符号整数使用32位前31位表示整数值，第32位表示数值的符号，这一位称为<strong>符号位</strong>，他的值决定了数值其余部分的格式。</p>
<p>布尔操作符：逻辑与&amp;&amp;（短路操作符）、逻辑或||、逻辑非!</p>
<p>乘性操作符：乘法*、除法/、取模%</p>
<p>指数操作符：Math.pow(底数，指数)</p>
<p>加性操作符：加法+、减法-</p>
<p>关系操作符：小于&lt;、大于&gt;~~~</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>3.6语句</strong></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>if语句</strong>：</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb16"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb16-1"><a href="#cb16-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">if</span>(i<span class="op">&gt;</span><span class="dv">18</span>){</span>
<span id="cb16-2"><a href="#cb16-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;成年了！&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb16-3"><a href="#cb16-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="cf">else</span> <span class="cf">if</span>(i<span class="op">&gt;</span><span class="dv">22</span>){</span>
<span id="cb16-4"><a href="#cb16-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    soncole<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;大学毕业了！&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb16-5"><a href="#cb16-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="cf">else</span>{</span>
<span id="cb16-6"><a href="#cb16-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;找工作了！&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb16-7"><a href="#cb16-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>

class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb17-1"><a href="#cb17-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> i <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb17-2"><a href="#cb17-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>  <span class="cf">do</span>{</span>

class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb18-1"><a href="#cb18-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> i <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb18-2"><a href="#cb18-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">while</span>(i<span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dv">10</span>){</span>

<p><strong>for语句</strong>:</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb19"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb19-1"><a href="#cb19-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span>(<span class="kw">let</span> i <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">;</span>i<span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">;</span>i<span class="op">++</span>){</span>
<span id="cb19-2"><a href="#cb19-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(i)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb19-3"><a href="#cb19-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>for-in语句</strong>：for(property in windows )
statment，用于枚举对象中的非符号键属性，每次循环都给变量property
赋予一个 windows对象的属性作为值，直到所有属性都被枚举一遍。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb20"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb20-1"><a href="#cb20-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span>(<span class="kw">const</span> propName <span class="kw">in</span> windows){</span>
<span id="cb20-2"><a href="#cb20-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(propName)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb20-3"><a href="#cb20-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="co">//表示每次执行循环，都会给变量propName赋予一个windows对象的属性作为值，直到windows的所有属性都被枚举一遍。</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>for-of语句</strong>：for(const el of
[1,3,5,7])，用于遍历可迭代对象的元素，循环会持续到所有元素都别迭代完。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb21"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb21-1"><a href="#cb21-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span>(<span class="kw">const</span> el <span class="kw">of</span> [<span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">3</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">5</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">7</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">9</span>]){</span>
<span id="cb21-2"><a href="#cb21-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(el)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//以此输出1,3,5，7,9</span></span>
<span id="cb21-3"><a href="#cb21-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>for in 和 for of 的区别:</strong></p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb22"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb22-1"><a href="#cb22-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">var</span> a <span class="op">=</span> [<span class="st">&quot;a&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;b&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;c&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;d&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;e&quot;</span>]<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-2"><a href="#cb22-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span> (<span class="kw">var</span> idx <span class="kw">in</span> a) {<span class="co">//建议 循环对象属性 的时候使用。</span></span>
<span id="cb22-3"><a href="#cb22-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>( idx )<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-4"><a href="#cb22-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb22-5"><a href="#cb22-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 0 1 2 3 4   for..in 在数组 a 的键 / 索引上循环。</span></span>
<span id="cb22-6"><a href="#cb22-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span> (<span class="kw">var</span> val <span class="kw">of</span> a) {<span class="co">//建议 遍历数组 的时候使用</span></span>
<span id="cb22-7"><a href="#cb22-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>( val )<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb22-8"><a href="#cb22-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb22-9"><a href="#cb22-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// &quot;a&quot; &quot;b&quot; &quot;c&quot; &quot;d&quot; &quot;e&quot;   而 for..of 在 a 的 值 上循环。</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>①在底层，for..of 循环向 iterable
请求一个迭代器，然后反复调用这个迭代器把它产生的值赋给循环迭代变量。---《你不知道的JavaScript-下卷》</p>
<p>②for..of可以通过break、continue、return
提前终止，并抛出异常。---《你不知道的JavaScript-下卷》</p>
<p><strong>break 和 continue的区别</strong>：</p>
<p><strong>break语句</strong>：跳出当前循环，执行循环后的下一条语句；</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb23"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb23-1"><a href="#cb23-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb23-2"><a href="#cb23-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span>(<span class="kw">let</span> i <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">;</span>i<span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">;</span>i<span class="op">++</span>){</span>
<span id="cb23-3"><a href="#cb23-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span>(i<span class="op">%</span><span class="dv">5</span><span class="op">==</span><span class="dv">0</span>){</span>
<span id="cb23-4"><a href="#cb23-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">break</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb23-5"><a href="#cb23-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb23-6"><a href="#cb23-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    num<span class="op">++;</span></span>
<span id="cb23-7"><a href="#cb23-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb23-8"><a href="#cb23-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(num)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//结果是4,为什么？</span></span>
<span id="cb23-9"><a href="#cb23-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                 <span class="co">//因为循环体递增到i能够被5取模的时候，循环体已经跳出了，num没有继续+1</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>continue语句</strong>：退出循环后，再次回到循环顶部重新开始执行。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb24"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb24-1"><a href="#cb24-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">;</span> </span>
<span id="cb24-2"><a href="#cb24-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">for</span>(<span class="kw">let</span> i <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">;</span>i<span class="op">&lt;</span><span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">;</span>i<span class="op">++</span>){</span>
<span id="cb24-3"><a href="#cb24-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span>(i<span class="op">%</span><span class="dv">5</span><span class="op">==</span><span class="dv">0</span>){</span>
<span id="cb24-4"><a href="#cb24-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(num)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb24-5"><a href="#cb24-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">continue</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb24-6"><a href="#cb24-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb24-7"><a href="#cb24-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    num<span class="op">++;</span></span>
<span id="cb24-8"><a href="#cb24-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(num)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb24-9"><a href="#cb24-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb24-10"><a href="#cb24-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(num)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//结果是8，为什么？</span></span>
<span id="cb24-11"><a href="#cb24-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                 <span class="co">//因为循环体递增到i能够被5取模的时候，遇到continue跳出，再次回到循环顶部重新执行了一遍，</span></span>
<span id="cb24-12"><a href="#cb24-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                 <span class="co">//又因为0%5和1%5都等于1，所以最终结果为8。</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>switch语句</strong>：</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb25"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb25-1"><a href="#cb25-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">switch</span>(i){</span>
<span id="cb25-2"><a href="#cb25-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">case</span> <span class="dv">25</span><span class="op">:</span></span>
<span id="cb25-3"><a href="#cb25-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;25&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-4"><a href="#cb25-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        borek<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-5"><a href="#cb25-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">case</span> <span class="dv">35</span><span class="op">:</span></span>
<span id="cb25-6"><a href="#cb25-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;35&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-7"><a href="#cb25-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        borek<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-8"><a href="#cb25-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">case</span> <span class="dv">45</span><span class="op">:</span></span>
<span id="cb25-9"><a href="#cb25-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;45&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-10"><a href="#cb25-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        borek<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-11"><a href="#cb25-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">case</span> <span class="dv">55</span><span class="op">:</span></span>
<span id="cb25-12"><a href="#cb25-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>         <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;55&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-13"><a href="#cb25-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>         borek<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-14"><a href="#cb25-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">default</span><span class="op">:</span></span>
<span id="cb25-15"><a href="#cb25-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;Outher&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb25-16"><a href="#cb25-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>With语句</strong>：用于设置代码在特定对象中的作用域</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb26"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb26-1"><a href="#cb26-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">var</span> sMessage <span class="op">=</span><span class="st">&quot;hello kuishou&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb26-2"><a href="#cb26-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="cf">with</span>(sMessage){</span>
<span id="cb26-3"><a href="#cb26-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">alert</span>(<span class="fu">toUpperCase</span>())<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//</span></span>
<span id="cb26-4"><a href="#cb26-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>

<li><strong>3.7函数</strong></li>
</ul>

<div class="sourceCode" id="cb27"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb27-1"><a href="#cb27-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">diff</span>(num1<span class="op">,</span>num2){<span class="co">//diff()函数用于计算两个数值的差</span></span>
<span id="cb27-2"><a href="#cb27-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span>(num1<span class="op">&lt;</span>num2){</span>
<span id="cb27-3"><a href="#cb27-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">return</span> num2 <span class="op">-</span> num1<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb27-4"><a href="#cb27-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }<span class="cf">else</span>{</span>
<span id="cb27-5"><a href="#cb27-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">return</span> num1<span class="op">-</span>num2<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb27-6"><a href="#cb27-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>

<h3 id="第4章变量作用域与内存">第4章——变量、作用域与内存</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>4.1传递参数</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb28"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb28-1"><a href="#cb28-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">addTen</span>(num){</span>
<span id="cb28-2"><a href="#cb28-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    num <span class="op">+=</span><span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-3"><a href="#cb28-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">return</span> num<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-4"><a href="#cb28-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb28-5"><a href="#cb28-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> count <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">20</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-6"><a href="#cb28-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> result <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fu">addTen</span>(count)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-7"><a href="#cb28-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(count)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//20</span></span>
<span id="cb28-8"><a href="#cb28-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(result)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//30</span></span>
<span id="cb28-9"><a href="#cb28-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb28-10"><a href="#cb28-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">setName</span>(obj) {</span>
<span id="cb28-11"><a href="#cb28-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    obj<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">name</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;kuishou&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-12"><a href="#cb28-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    obj <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Object</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-13"><a href="#cb28-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    obj<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">name</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;jianlin&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-14"><a href="#cb28-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb28-15"><a href="#cb28-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> person <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Object</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-16"><a href="#cb28-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">setName</span>(person)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb28-17"><a href="#cb28-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(person<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">name</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//kuishou</span></span></code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><strong>4.2执行上下文与作用域。</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>每个上下文都有一个关联的<strong>变量对象</strong>,这个上下文中定义的所有变量和函数都存在于这个对象上。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb29"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb29-1"><a href="#cb29-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">var</span> color <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;blue&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb29-2"><a href="#cb29-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">changeColor</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb29-3"><a href="#cb29-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span>(color <span class="op">===</span> <span class="st">&quot;blue&quot;</span>){</span>
<span id="cb29-4"><a href="#cb29-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        color <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;red&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb29-5"><a href="#cb29-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb29-6"><a href="#cb29-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb29-7"><a href="#cb29-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">changeColor</span>()<span class="op">;</span>     <span class="co">//这个函数的作用域包含两个对象：所以能把red显示在全局变量中</span></span>
<span id="cb29-8"><a href="#cb29-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(color)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//red</span></span></code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>4.3垃圾回收</strong></p>
<p>确定某个变量不会再使用，然后释放它占用的内存，周期性清理，属于’不判定的‘问题。</p>
<p>两种标记策略：标记清理、引用计数。</p></li>
</ul>
<p>​<strong>标记清理</strong>流程：声明一个变量时，这个变量就会被加上
**存在于上下文
**的标记，垃圾回收程序运行的时候，被加上标记的变量就是待删除变量，随后垃圾回收程序做一次内存清理，销毁带标记的所有值并回收他们的内存。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb30"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb30-1"><a href="#cb30-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">functiontest</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb30-2"><a href="#cb30-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> vara <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">10</span> <span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">//被标记</span></span>
<span id="cb30-3"><a href="#cb30-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> ，进入环境</span>
<span id="cb30-4"><a href="#cb30-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> varb <span class="op">=</span> <span class="dv">20</span> <span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">//被标记</span></span>
<span id="cb30-5"><a href="#cb30-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> ，进入环境</span>
<span id="cb30-6"><a href="#cb30-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb30-7"><a href="#cb30-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">test</span>()<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//执行完毕</span></span>
<span id="cb30-8"><a href="#cb30-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> 之后 a、b又被标离开环境，被回收。</span></code></pre></div>
<p>​
<strong>引用计数</strong>：对每个值都记录它被引用的次数，变量被引用一次，那么引用数+1；变量被其他值覆盖，引用值-1；当引用值为0的时候，回收其内存。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb31"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb31-1"><a href="#cb31-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">functiontest</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb31-2"><a href="#cb31-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> vara <span class="op">=</span> {} <span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">//a的引用次数为0</span></span>
<span id="cb31-3"><a href="#cb31-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> varb <span class="op">=</span> a <span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">//a的引用次数加1，为1</span></span>
<span id="cb31-4"><a href="#cb31-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> varc <span class="op">=</span>a<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">//a的引用次数再加1，为2</span></span>
<span id="cb31-5"><a href="#cb31-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> varb <span class="op">=</span>{}<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">//a的引用次数减1，为1</span></span>
<span id="cb31-6"><a href="#cb31-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span></code></pre></div>
<hr />
<h3 id="第5章基本引用类型">第5章——基本引用类型</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>5.1 Date 类型</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb32"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb32-1"><a href="#cb32-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> now <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Date</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb32-2"><a href="#cb32-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(now)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//Tue Mar 23 2021 18:03:19 GMT+0800 (中国标准时间)</span></span></code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><strong>5.2 RegExp 正则表达式</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb33"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb33-1"><a href="#cb33-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// g：全局模式，表示查找字符串的全部内容，而不是找到第一个匹配的内容就结束。</span></span>
<span id="cb33-2"><a href="#cb33-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// i：不区分大小写，表示在查找匹配时忽略 pattern 和字符串的大小写。</span></span>
<span id="cb33-3"><a href="#cb33-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// m：多行模式，表示查找到一行文本末尾时会继续查找。</span></span>
<span id="cb33-4"><a href="#cb33-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// y：粘附模式，表示只查找从 lastIndex 开始及之后的字符串。</span></span>
<span id="cb33-5"><a href="#cb33-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// u：Unicode 模式，启用 Unicode 匹配。</span></span>
<span id="cb33-6"><a href="#cb33-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// s：dotAll 模式，表示元字符.匹配任何字符（包括\n 或\r）。</span></span>
<span id="cb33-7"><a href="#cb33-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 匹配字符串中的所有&quot;at&quot;</span></span>
<span id="cb33-8"><a href="#cb33-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> pattern1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="ss">/at/g</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb33-9"><a href="#cb33-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 匹配第一个&quot;bat&quot;或&quot;cat&quot;，忽略大小写</span></span>
<span id="cb33-10"><a href="#cb33-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> pattern2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="ss">/</span><span class="sc">[bc]</span><span class="ss">at/i</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb33-11"><a href="#cb33-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 匹配所有以&quot;at&quot;结尾的三字符组合，忽略大小写</span></span>
<span id="cb33-12"><a href="#cb33-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> pattern3 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="ss">/.at/gi</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb33-13"><a href="#cb33-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 匹配第一个&quot;bat&quot;或&quot;cat&quot;，忽略大小写</span></span>
<span id="cb33-14"><a href="#cb33-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> pattern1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="ss">/</span><span class="sc">[bc]</span><span class="ss">at/i</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb33-15"><a href="#cb33-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 匹配第一个&quot;[bc]at&quot;，忽略大小写</span></span>
<span id="cb33-16"><a href="#cb33-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> pattern2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="ss">/</span><span class="sc">\[</span><span class="ss">bc</span><span class="sc">\]</span><span class="ss">at/i</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb33-17"><a href="#cb33-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 匹配所有以&quot;at&quot;结尾的三字符组合，忽略大小写</span></span>
<span id="cb33-18"><a href="#cb33-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> pattern3 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="ss">/.at/gi</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb33-19"><a href="#cb33-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 匹配所有&quot;.at&quot;，忽略大小写</span></span></code></pre></div>

<span id="cb36-8"><a href="#cb36-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(stringValue<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">slice</span>(<span class="dv">3</span><span class="op">,-</span><span class="dv">4</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//llo kui，从右边开始，返回3-7这个区间内所有的字符串</span></span>
<span id="cb36-9"><a href="#cb36-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb36-10"><a href="#cb36-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(stringValue<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">indexOf</span>(<span class="st">&quot;o&quot;</span>))<span class="co">//4,从左边开始，找出字母o所在的位置</span></span>
<span id="cb36-11"><a href="#cb36-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(stringValue<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">lastIndexOf</span>(<span class="st">&quot;o&quot;</span>))<span class="co">//11,从左边开始，找出字母o所在的位置</span></span>
<span id="cb36-12"><a href="#cb36-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(stringValue<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">indexOf</span>(<span class="st">&quot;o&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">6</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//11,从位置6（字符k）开始向后开始搜索，在位置11找到了o</span></span>
<span id="cb36-13"><a href="#cb36-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(stringValue<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">lastIndexOf</span>(<span class="st">&quot;o&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">6</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//4,从位置6（字符k）开始反向开始搜索，在位置4找到了o</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>trim()方法</strong>：创建字符串的一个副本，删除前后所有空格符，再返回起结果。</p>

class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb37-1"><a href="#cb37-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> stringValue <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot; hello world &quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>

class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb38-1"><a href="#cb38-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> stringValue <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;na &quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>

<li><strong>5.4 Math</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb39"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb39-1"><a href="#cb39-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> max <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">max</span>(<span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">2</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">3</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">4</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">5</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb39-3"><a href="#cb39-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb39-4"><a href="#cb39-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> min <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">min</span>(<span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">2</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">3</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">4</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">5</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>

<p>**Math.round()**方法执行四舍五入</p>
<p><strong>Math.ceil()方法</strong>：始终向上舍入最接近的整数。</p>
<p><strong>Math.floor()方法</strong>：始终向下舍入最接近的整数。</p>
<p><strong>Math.round()方法</strong>：执行四舍五入。</p>
<p><strong>Math.fround()方法</strong>：返回数值最接近的单精度（32位）浮点值表示。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb40"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb40-1"><a href="#cb40-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">ceil</span>(<span class="fl">25.9</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//26,向上取整</span></span>
<span id="cb40-2"><a href="#cb40-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">ceil</span>(<span class="fl">25.5</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//26</span></span>
<span id="cb40-3"><a href="#cb40-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">ceil</span>(<span class="fl">25.4</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//26</span></span>
<span id="cb40-4"><a href="#cb40-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">ceil</span>(<span class="fl">25.1</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//26</span></span>
<span id="cb40-5"><a href="#cb40-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-6"><a href="#cb40-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">floor</span>(<span class="fl">25.9</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25，向下取整</span></span>
<span id="cb40-7"><a href="#cb40-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">floor</span>(<span class="fl">25.5</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25</span></span>
<span id="cb40-8"><a href="#cb40-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">floor</span>(<span class="fl">25.4</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25</span></span>
<span id="cb40-9"><a href="#cb40-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">floor</span>(<span class="fl">25.1</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25</span></span>
<span id="cb40-10"><a href="#cb40-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-11"><a href="#cb40-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">round</span>(<span class="fl">25.9</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//26，四舍五入</span></span>
<span id="cb40-12"><a href="#cb40-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">round</span>(<span class="fl">25.5</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//26</span></span>
<span id="cb40-13"><a href="#cb40-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">round</span>(<span class="fl">25.4</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25</span></span>
<span id="cb40-14"><a href="#cb40-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">round</span>(<span class="fl">25.1</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25</span></span>
<span id="cb40-15"><a href="#cb40-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb40-16"><a href="#cb40-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">fround</span>(<span class="fl">25.9</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25.899999618530273，返回数值最接近的单精度浮点值</span></span>
<span id="cb40-17"><a href="#cb40-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">fround</span>(<span class="fl">25.5</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25.5</span></span>
<span id="cb40-18"><a href="#cb40-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">fround</span>(<span class="fl">25.4</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25.399999618530273</span></span>
<span id="cb40-19"><a href="#cb40-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">fround</span>(<span class="fl">25.1</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//25.100000381469727</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>**Math.random()**生成随机数。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb41"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb41-1"><a href="#cb41-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">floor</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">random</span>()<span class="op">*</span><span class="dv">10</span><span class="op">+</span><span class="dv">1</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb41-2"><a href="#cb41-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(num)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//1~10范围内的随机数</span></span>
<span id="cb41-3"><a href="#cb41-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb41-4"><a href="#cb41-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">/*-------------------------- */</span></span>
<span id="cb41-5"><a href="#cb41-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">selectFrom</span>(lowerValue<span class="op">,</span>upperValue){</span>
<span id="cb41-6"><a href="#cb41-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">let</span> choices <span class="op">=</span> upperValue <span class="op">-</span> lowerValue <span class="op">+</span> <span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb41-7"><a href="#cb41-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">floor</span>(<span class="bu">Math</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">random</span>() <span class="op">*</span> choices <span class="op">+</span> lowerValue)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb41-8"><a href="#cb41-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb41-9"><a href="#cb41-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> num <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fu">selectFrom</span>(<span class="dv">2</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">10</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb41-10"><a href="#cb41-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(num)<span class="op">;</span>   <span class="co">//2~10范围内的随机数</span></span>
<span id="cb41-11"><a href="#cb41-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb41-12"><a href="#cb41-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">/*-------------------------- */</span></span>
<span id="cb41-13"><a href="#cb41-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> colors <span class="op">=</span> [<span class="st">&quot;red&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;green&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;blue&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;black&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;brown&quot;</span>]<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb41-14"><a href="#cb41-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> color <span class="op">=</span> [<span class="fu">selectFrom</span>(<span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">,</span>colors<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">length</span><span class="op">-</span><span class="dv">1</span>)]<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb41-15"><a href="#cb41-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(color)<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<hr />
<h3 id="第6章集合应用类型">第6章——集合应用类型</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>6.1 Object</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>object适合存储和在应用程序之间交换数据。</p>
<p><strong>对象字面量</strong>：对象定义的简写形式，目的是为了简化包含大量属性的对象的创建。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb42"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb42-1"><a href="#cb42-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> person <span class="op">=</span>{<span class="co">//对象字面量 表示法</span></span>
<span id="cb42-2"><a href="#cb42-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">name</span> <span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;kuishou&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb42-3"><a href="#cb42-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">age</span> <span class="op">:</span> <span class="dv">21</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb42-4"><a href="#cb42-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">sex</span> <span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;男&quot;</span></span>
<span id="cb42-5"><a href="#cb42-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb42-6"><a href="#cb42-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb42-7"><a href="#cb42-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">displayInfo</span>(args){</span>
<span id="cb42-8"><a href="#cb42-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">let</span> output <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb42-9"><a href="#cb42-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span>(<span class="kw">typeof</span> args<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">name</span> <span class="op">==</span> <span class="st">&quot;string&quot;</span>){</span>
<span id="cb42-10"><a href="#cb42-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        output <span class="op">+=</span> <span class="st">&quot;Name:&quot;</span> <span class="op">+</span> args<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">name</span> <span class="op">+</span> <span class="st">&quot;</span><span class="sc">\n</span><span class="st">&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb42-11"><a href="#cb42-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb42-12"><a href="#cb42-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span>(<span class="kw">typeof</span> args<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">age</span>  <span class="op">==</span> <span class="st">&quot;number&quot;</span>){</span>
<span id="cb42-13"><a href="#cb42-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        output <span class="op">+=</span> <span class="st">&quot;Age: &quot;</span> <span class="op">+</span> args<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">age</span> <span class="op">+</span> <span class="st">&quot;</span><span class="sc">\n</span><span class="st">&quot;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb42-14"><a href="#cb42-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb42-15"><a href="#cb42-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">alert</span>(output)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//Name:kuishou Age:21</span></span>
<span id="cb42-16"><a href="#cb42-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb42-17"><a href="#cb42-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb42-18"><a href="#cb42-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">displayInfo</span>({</span>
<span id="cb42-19"><a href="#cb42-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">name</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;kuishou&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb42-20"><a href="#cb42-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">age</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="dv">21</span></span>
<span id="cb42-21"><a href="#cb42-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb42-22"><a href="#cb42-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb42-23"><a href="#cb42-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">displayInfo</span>({</span>
<span id="cb42-24"><a href="#cb42-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">name</span><span class="op">:</span> <span class="st">&quot;lingxiu&quot;</span></span>
<span id="cb42-25"><a href="#cb42-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>6.2 Array 数组</strong></p>
<p>创建数组</p></li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb43"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb43-1"><a href="#cb43-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> colors <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Array</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb43-2"><a href="#cb43-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> colors <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Array</span>(<span class="st">&quot;red&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;blue&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;black&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb43-3"><a href="#cb43-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> colors <span class="op">=</span> [<span class="st">&quot;red&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;green&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;black&quot;</span>]<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb44"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb44-1"><a href="#cb44-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//Array.from()拆分、合并数组</span></span>
<span id="cb44-2"><a href="#cb44-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Array</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">from</span>(<span class="st">&quot;kuishou&quot;</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//[&quot;k&quot;, &quot;u&quot;, &quot;i&quot;, &quot;s&quot;, &quot;h&quot;, &quot;o&quot;, &quot;u&quot;],拆分数组</span></span>
<span id="cb44-3"><a href="#cb44-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb44-4"><a href="#cb44-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> s <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Set</span>()<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">add</span>(<span class="dv">1</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">add</span>(<span class="dv">2</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">add</span>(<span class="dv">3</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">add</span>(<span class="dv">5</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">add</span>(<span class="dv">4</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb44-5"><a href="#cb44-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Array</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">from</span>(s))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//[1, 2, 3, 5, 4]，合并数组</span></span>
<span id="cb44-6"><a href="#cb44-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb44-7"><a href="#cb44-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> m <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Map</span>()<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">set</span>(<span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">2</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">set</span>(<span class="dv">3</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">4</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb44-8"><a href="#cb44-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Array</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">from</span>(m))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//[[1,2],[3,4]]，合并二维数组</span></span>
<span id="cb44-9"><a href="#cb44-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb44-10"><a href="#cb44-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//Array.of()把一组参数转换为数组</span></span>
<span id="cb44-11"><a href="#cb44-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Array</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">of</span>(<span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">2</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">3</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">4</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">5</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//[1, 2, 3, 4, 5]</span></span>
<span id="cb44-12"><a href="#cb44-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="bu">Array</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">of</span>(red<span class="op">,</span>black<span class="op">,</span>green))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//[&quot;red&quot;, &quot;black&quot;,&quot;green&quot;]</span></span>
