<span id="cb65-8"><a href="#cb65-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(proxy<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span>)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// target</span></span>
<span id="cb65-9"><a href="#cb65-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 给目标属性赋值会反映在两个对象上</span></span>
<span id="cb65-10"><a href="#cb65-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 因为两个对象访问的是同一个值</span></span>
<span id="cb65-11"><a href="#cb65-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>target<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;foo&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb65-12"><a href="#cb65-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(target<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span>)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// foo</span></span>
<span id="cb65-13"><a href="#cb65-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(proxy<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span>)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// foo</span></span>
<span id="cb65-14"><a href="#cb65-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 给代理属性赋值会反映在两个对象上</span></span>
<span id="cb65-15"><a href="#cb65-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 因为这个赋值会转移到目标对象</span></span>
<span id="cb65-16"><a href="#cb65-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>proxy<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;bar&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb65-17"><a href="#cb65-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(target<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span>)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// bar</span></span>
<span id="cb65-18"><a href="#cb65-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(proxy<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">id</span>)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// bar</span></span>
<span id="cb65-19"><a href="#cb65-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// hasOwnProperty()方法在两个地方</span></span>
<span id="cb65-20"><a href="#cb65-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 都会应用到目标对象</span></span>
<span id="cb65-21"><a href="#cb65-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(target<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">hasOwnProperty</span>(<span class="st">&#39;id&#39;</span>))<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// true</span></span>
<span id="cb65-22"><a href="#cb65-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(proxy<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">hasOwnProperty</span>(<span class="st">&#39;id&#39;</span>))<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// true</span></span>
<span id="cb65-23"><a href="#cb65-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// Proxy.prototype 是 undefined</span></span>
<span id="cb65-24"><a href="#cb65-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 因此不能使用 instanceof 操作符</span></span>
<span id="cb65-25"><a href="#cb65-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(target <span class="kw">instanceof</span> <span class="bu">Proxy</span>)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// TypeError: Function has non-object prototype</span></span>
<span id="cb65-26"><a href="#cb65-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="st">&#39;undefined&#39;</span> <span class="kw">in</span> <span class="kw">instanceof</span> check</span>
<span id="cb65-27"><a href="#cb65-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(proxy <span class="kw">instanceof</span> <span class="bu">Proxy</span>)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// TypeError: Function has non-object prototype</span></span>
<span id="cb65-28"><a href="#cb65-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="st">&#39;undefined&#39;</span> <span class="kw">in</span> <span class="kw">instanceof</span> check</span>
<span id="cb65-29"><a href="#cb65-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">// 严格相等可以用来区分代理和目标</span></span>
<span id="cb65-30"><a href="#cb65-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(target <span class="op">===</span> proxy)<span class="op">;</span> <span class="co">// false</span></span></code></pre></div>
<hr />
<h3 id="第10章函数">第10章——函数</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>10.1 箭头函数</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb66"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb66-1"><a href="#cb66-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> arrowSum <span class="op">=</span> (a<span class="op">,</span>b) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {<span class="co">//箭头函数</span></span>
<span id="cb66-2"><a href="#cb66-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">return</span> a<span class="op">+</span>b<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb66-3"><a href="#cb66-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb66-4"><a href="#cb66-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> functionExpressionSum <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">function</span> (a<span class="op">,</span>b) {<span class="co">//普通函数</span></span>
<span id="cb66-5"><a href="#cb66-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">return</span> a<span class="op">+</span>b<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb66-6"><a href="#cb66-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb66-7"><a href="#cb66-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="fu">arrowSum</span>(<span class="dv">6</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">8</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//14</span></span>
<span id="cb66-8"><a href="#cb66-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="fu">functionExpressionSum</span>(<span class="dv">6</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">8</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//14</span></span></code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><strong>10.2 函数内部</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>arguments对象：是一个类数组对象（第一个参数是arguments[0],第二个参数是arguments[1])。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb67"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb67-1"><a href="#cb67-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">doAdd</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb67-2"><a href="#cb67-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span>(<span class="kw">arguments</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">length</span><span class="op">==</span><span class="dv">1</span>){</span>
<span id="cb67-3"><a href="#cb67-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="kw">arguments</span>[<span class="dv">0</span>]<span class="op">+</span><span class="dv">10</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb67-4"><a href="#cb67-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }<span class="cf">else</span> <span class="cf">if</span>(<span class="kw">arguments</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">length</span><span class="op">==</span><span class="dv">2</span>){</span>
<span id="cb67-5"><a href="#cb67-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="kw">arguments</span>[<span class="dv">0</span>]<span class="op">+</span><span class="kw">arguments</span>[<span class="dv">1</span>])<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb67-6"><a href="#cb67-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb67-7"><a href="#cb67-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb67-8"><a href="#cb67-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">doAdd</span>(<span class="dv">10</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//20</span></span>
<span id="cb67-9"><a href="#cb67-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">doAdd</span>(<span class="dv">20</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">30</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//50</span></span>
<span id="cb67-10"><a href="#cb67-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb67-11"><a href="#cb67-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> trueFactorial <span class="op">=</span> factorial<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb67-12"><a href="#cb67-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>factorial <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">function</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb67-13"><a href="#cb67-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb67-14"><a href="#cb67-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb67-15"><a href="#cb67-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="fu">trueFactorial</span>(<span class="dv">5</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//120</span></span>
<span id="cb67-16"><a href="#cb67-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="fu">factorial</span>(<span class="dv">5</span>))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//0</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>this
对象：在标准函数中，this引用的是把函数当成方法调用的上下文对象。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb68"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb68-1"><a href="#cb68-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">window</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">coloe</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;red&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-2"><a href="#cb68-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> o <span class="op">=</span>{</span>
<span id="cb68-3"><a href="#cb68-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">color</span><span class="op">:</span><span class="st">&#39;bule&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-4"><a href="#cb68-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-5"><a href="#cb68-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">sayColor</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb68-6"><a href="#cb68-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">coolor</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-7"><a href="#cb68-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb68-8"><a href="#cb68-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">sayColor</span>()<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//&#39;red&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-9"><a href="#cb68-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb68-10"><a href="#cb68-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>o<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">sayColor</span> <span class="op">=</span> sayColor<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-11"><a href="#cb68-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>o<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">sayColor</span>()<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//&#39;blue&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-12"><a href="#cb68-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb68-13"><a href="#cb68-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//this 在箭头函数中，this引用的是定义箭头函数的上下文。</span></span>
<span id="cb68-14"><a href="#cb68-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>windows<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">color</span> <span class="op">=</span> <span class="st">&#39;red&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-15"><a href="#cb68-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> o <span class="op">=</span>{</span>
<span id="cb68-16"><a href="#cb68-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="dt">color</span><span class="op">:</span><span class="st">&#39;blue&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-17"><a href="#cb68-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-18"><a href="#cb68-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> sayColor <span class="op">=</span> () <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="kw">this</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="at">color</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-19"><a href="#cb68-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">sayColor</span>()<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//&#39;red&#39;</span></span>
<span id="cb68-20"><a href="#cb68-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>o<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">sayColor</span> <span class="op">=</span> sayColor<span class="op">;</span></span>

<ul>
<li><strong>10.3 递归</strong> ：一个函数通过名称自己调用自己。</li>
</ul>
<p>arguments.callee 指向一个正在执行的函数的指针。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb69"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb69-1"><a href="#cb69-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">factorial</span>(num){</span>

<span id="cb69-3"><a href="#cb69-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb69-4"><a href="#cb69-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    } <span class="cf">else</span> {</span>
<span id="cb69-5"><a href="#cb69-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">return</span> num<span class="op">*</span><span class="kw">arguments</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">callee</span>(num<span class="op">-</span><span class="dv">1</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb69-6"><a href="#cb69-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb69-7"><a href="#cb69-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>

<span id="cb69-9"><a href="#cb69-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> factorial <span class="op">=</span> (<span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">f</span>(num){</span>
<span id="cb69-10"><a href="#cb69-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">if</span> (num<span class="op">&lt;=</span><span class="dv">1</span>){</span>
<span id="cb69-11"><a href="#cb69-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="dv">1</span><span class="op">;</span></span>

<h3 id="第11章期约与异步函数">第11章——期约与异步函数</h3>
<ul>
<li>11.2 <strong>期约（promise）</strong>:是对 尚不存在结果
的一个替身。</li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb72"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb72-1"><a href="#cb72-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">/**</span></span>
<span id="cb72-2"><a href="#cb72-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 期约与异步函数</span></span>
<span id="cb72-3"><a href="#cb72-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 什么是Promise?</span></span>
<span id="cb72-4"><a href="#cb72-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （1）从语法上来说：Promise是一个构造函数</span></span>
<span id="cb72-5"><a href="#cb72-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （2）从功能上来说：Promise对象用来封装一个异步操作并获取其结果。</span></span>
<span id="cb72-6"><a href="#cb72-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * Promise基本远行流程</span></span>
<span id="cb72-7"><a href="#cb72-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （1）创建一个新的Promise 对象</span></span>
<span id="cb72-8"><a href="#cb72-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （2) 执行异步操作任务</span></span>
<span id="cb72-9"><a href="#cb72-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （3）异步任务成功则返回resolve(),失败则返回reject()</span></span>
<span id="cb72-10"><a href="#cb72-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （4）resolved状态通过then()回调onResolved();rejected状态通过then()/catch()回调onReject()</span></span>
<span id="cb72-11"><a href="#cb72-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （5）最后形成一个新的Promise对象</span></span>
<span id="cb72-12"><a href="#cb72-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> */</span></span>
<span id="cb72-13"><a href="#cb72-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//失败处理</span></span>

<span id="cb72-15"><a href="#cb72-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(() <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>

<span id="cb72-18"><a href="#cb72-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                <span class="cf">throw</span> <span class="st">&#39;Must provide number as firdt argument&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb72-19"><a href="#cb72-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            }</span>
<span id="cb72-20"><a href="#cb72-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="fu">success</span>(<span class="dv">2</span> <span class="op">*</span> value)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb72-21"><a href="#cb72-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        }<span class="cf">catch</span>(e){</span>
<span id="cb72-22"><a href="#cb72-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="fu">failure</span>(e)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb72-23"><a href="#cb72-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        }</span>
<span id="cb72-24"><a href="#cb72-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }<span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">1000</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb72-25"><a href="#cb72-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>

<span id="cb72-27"><a href="#cb72-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> successCallback <span class="op">=</span> (x) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;Success：${x}&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb72-28"><a href="#cb72-28" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> failureCallback <span class="op">=</span> (e) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;Failure：${e}&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb72-32"><a href="#cb72-32" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>

<span id="cb72-47"><a href="#cb72-47" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> successCallback <span class="op">=</span> (x) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>

<span id="cb72-50"><a href="#cb72-50" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> failureCallback <span class="op">=</span> (e) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;Failure:${e}&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb72-51"><a href="#cb72-51" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">double</span>(<span class="dv">3</span><span class="op">,</span>successCallback<span class="op">,</span>failureCallback)<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>Promise 对象状态改变的方式：</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb73"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb73-1"><a href="#cb73-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//1.声明一个Promise对象的状态</span></span>
<span id="cb73-2"><a href="#cb73-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb73-3"><a href="#cb73-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="co">//resolve 函数</span></span>
<span id="cb73-4"><a href="#cb73-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">resolve</span>(<span class="st">&#39;OK&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//pending =&gt;fulfilled(resolve)</span></span>
<span id="cb73-5"><a href="#cb73-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="co">//reject  函数</span></span>
<span id="cb73-6"><a href="#cb73-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">reject</span>(<span class="st">&#39;Error&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//pending =&gt; rejected</span></span>
<span id="cb73-7"><a href="#cb73-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="co">//抛出错误</span></span>
<span id="cb73-8"><a href="#cb73-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">throw</span> <span class="st">&#39;出问题了&#39;</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-9"><a href="#cb73-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-10"><a href="#cb73-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-11"><a href="#cb73-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb73-12"><a href="#cb73-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//Promise指定多个成功/失败回调函数，都会调用嘛？</span></span>
<span id="cb73-13"><a href="#cb73-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//当Promise改变为对应状态时，都会被调用</span></span>
<span id="cb73-14"><a href="#cb73-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb73-15"><a href="#cb73-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">resolve</span>(<span class="st">&#39;OK&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-16"><a href="#cb73-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-17"><a href="#cb73-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//指定回调</span></span>
<span id="cb73-18"><a href="#cb73-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>p<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(value <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb73-19"><a href="#cb73-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(value)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-20"><a href="#cb73-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-21"><a href="#cb73-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//指定回调</span></span>
<span id="cb73-22"><a href="#cb73-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>p<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(value <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb73-23"><a href="#cb73-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">alert</span>(value)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb73-24"><a href="#cb73-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>三种状态：待定（pending）、兑现(resovle)、拒绝(reject)</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb74"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb74-1"><a href="#cb74-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">/**</span></span>
<span id="cb74-2"><a href="#cb74-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * promise 期约是对尚不存在结果的一个替身</span></span>
<span id="cb74-3"><a href="#cb74-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 三种状态：待定（pending）、兑现（fulfilled,可以叫解决（resolve））、拒绝（rejected），三种状态不可逆</span></span>
<span id="cb74-4"><a href="#cb74-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 待定（pending）:期约的最初始状态。</span></span>
<span id="cb74-5"><a href="#cb74-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 兑现（fulfilled）:期约落定（settled）为代表成功状态</span></span>
<span id="cb74-6"><a href="#cb74-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 拒绝（rejected）:期约落定（settled）为代表失败状态</span></span>
<span id="cb74-7"><a href="#cb74-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 用途：抽象的表示一个异步操作；状态代表期约是否完成。</span></span>
<span id="cb74-8"><a href="#cb74-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> */</span></span>
<span id="cb74-9"><a href="#cb74-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>(() <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {})<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb74-10"><a href="#cb74-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(<span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">,</span>p)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb74-11"><a href="#cb74-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb74-12"><a href="#cb74-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="fu">resolve</span>())<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb74-13"><a href="#cb74-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(<span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="dv">0</span> <span class="op">,</span>p1)<span class="co">//Promise {&lt;fulfilled&gt;: undefined}</span></span>
<span id="cb74-14"><a href="#cb74-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb74-15"><a href="#cb74-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="fu">reject</span>())<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb74-16"><a href="#cb74-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(<span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="dv">0</span> <span class="op">,</span>p2)<span class="co">//Promise {&lt;rejected&gt;: undefined}</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>Promise.prototype.then()为Promise实例添加状态改变时的回调函数。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb75"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb75-1"><a href="#cb75-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//then方法返回的是一个新的Promise实例。</span></span>
<span id="cb75-2"><a href="#cb75-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">getJSON</span>(<span class="st">&quot;/post/1.json&quot;</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(</span>
<span id="cb75-3"><a href="#cb75-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    post <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="fu">getJSON</span>(post<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">commentURL</span>)</span>
<span id="cb75-4"><a href="#cb75-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(</span>
<span id="cb75-5"><a href="#cb75-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    comments <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;resolved:&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span>comments)<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb75-6"><a href="#cb75-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    err <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&quot;rejected:&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span>err)</span>
<span id="cb75-7"><a href="#cb75-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>)<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>Promise.prototype.catch() 发生错误时的回调函数。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb76"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb76-1"><a href="#cb76-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> somrAsyncThing <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">function</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb76-2"><a href="#cb76-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>(<span class="kw">function</span>(resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject){</span>
<span id="cb76-3"><a href="#cb76-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="fu">resolve</span>(x <span class="op">+</span> <span class="dv">2</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//会报错，因为x没有声明</span></span>
<span id="cb76-4"><a href="#cb76-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    })<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb76-5"><a href="#cb76-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb76-6"><a href="#cb76-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">somrAsyncThing</span>()<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">catch</span>(<span class="kw">function</span>(error){</span>
<span id="cb76-7"><a href="#cb76-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;error&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>error)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb76-8"><a href="#cb76-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(<span class="kw">function</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb76-9"><a href="#cb76-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;error&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb76-10"><a href="#cb76-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>Promise.prototype.finally()
不管Promise对象最后状态如何，都会执行的操作。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb77"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb77-1"><a href="#cb77-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">resolve</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb77-2"><a href="#cb77-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">reject</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb77-3"><a href="#cb77-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> onFinally <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">function</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb77-4"><a href="#cb77-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(<span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="dv">0</span><span class="op">,</span> <span class="st">&#39;Finally!&#39;</span>)</span>
<span id="cb77-5"><a href="#cb77-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb77-6"><a href="#cb77-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>p1<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">finally</span>(onFinally)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//Finally</span></span>
<span id="cb77-7"><a href="#cb77-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>p2<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">finally</span>(onFinally)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//Finally</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>Promise.all()
接收一个可迭代对象，返回一个新期约，在一组期约全部解决之后再解决。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb78"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb78-1"><a href="#cb78-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> p1 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb78-2"><a href="#cb78-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">resolve</span>(<span class="st">&quot;hello&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb78-3"><a href="#cb78-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(result <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> result)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb78-4"><a href="#cb78-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb78-5"><a href="#cb78-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> p2 <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb78-6"><a href="#cb78-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">throw</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Error</span>(<span class="st">&#39;error&#39;</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb78-7"><a href="#cb78-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(result <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> result)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb78-8"><a href="#cb78-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb78-9"><a href="#cb78-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">all</span>([p1<span class="op">,</span>p2])</span>
<span id="cb78-10"><a href="#cb78-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(result <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(result))</span>
<span id="cb78-11"><a href="#cb78-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">catch</span>(e <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(e))<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p>Promise.race() 将多个Promise实例，包装成一个新的Promise实例。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb79"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb79-1"><a href="#cb79-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> p <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">race</span>([p1<span class="op">,</span>p2<span class="op">,</span>p3])<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//只要有一个实例率先改变状态，P的转态就会发生改变</span></span>
<span id="cb79-2"><a href="#cb79-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">const</span> p <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">race</span>([</span>
<span id="cb79-3"><a href="#cb79-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">fetch</span>(<span class="st">&#39;/resource-that-may-take-a-while&#39;</span>)<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb79-4"><a href="#cb79-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>(<span class="kw">function</span>(resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject){</span>
<span id="cb79-5"><a href="#cb79-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(() <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="fu">reject</span>(<span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Error</span>(<span class="st">&#39;request timeout&#39;</span>))<span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">5000</span>)</span>
<span id="cb79-6"><a href="#cb79-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    })</span>
<span id="cb79-7"><a href="#cb79-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>])<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb79-8"><a href="#cb79-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>p<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(<span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">catch</span>(<span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">error</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span></code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><strong>11.3 异步函数</strong>：旨在解决利用异步结构
组织代码的问题</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>async关键字</strong>用于声明异步函数，它是Generator
函数的语法糖。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb80"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb80-1"><a href="#cb80-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">foo</span>(){}</span>
<span id="cb80-2"><a href="#cb80-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> bar <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span>(){}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb80-3"><a href="#cb80-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> baz <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">async</span> () <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {}<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb80-4"><a href="#cb80-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">class</span> Qux{</span>
<span id="cb80-5"><a href="#cb80-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="fu">qux</span>(){}</span>
<span id="cb80-6"><a href="#cb80-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb80-7"><a href="#cb80-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb80-8"><a href="#cb80-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> p <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((result<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(result<span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">1000</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">3</span>))<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb80-9"><a href="#cb80-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>p<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>((x) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(x))<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//3</span></span></code></pre></div>
<p><strong>await关键字</strong>用于暂停步函数代码的执行，等待期约解决。</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb81"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb81-1"><a href="#cb81-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">foo</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb81-2"><a href="#cb81-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="kw">let</span> p <span class="op">=</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span>reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> <span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(resolve<span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">1000</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="dv">3</span>))<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-3"><a href="#cb81-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="cf">await</span> p)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-4"><a href="#cb81-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb81-5"><a href="#cb81-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">foo</span>()<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//3</span></span>
<span id="cb81-6"><a href="#cb81-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb81-7"><a href="#cb81-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//停止和恢复执行</span></span>
<span id="cb81-8"><a href="#cb81-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">foo</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb81-9"><a href="#cb81-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="dv">2</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-10"><a href="#cb81-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="cf">await</span> <span class="kw">null</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-11"><a href="#cb81-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="dv">4</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-12"><a href="#cb81-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>}</span>
<span id="cb81-13"><a href="#cb81-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="dv">1</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-14"><a href="#cb81-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="fu">foo</span>()<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-15"><a href="#cb81-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="dv">3</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-16"><a href="#cb81-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//1</span></span>
<span id="cb81-17"><a href="#cb81-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//2,打印完2后，由于遇到arait关键字，null向消息队列添加一个任务，退出foo()</span></span>
<span id="cb81-18"><a href="#cb81-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//3.打印完3，再次回到foo()中恢复执行。</span></span>
<span id="cb81-19"><a href="#cb81-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">//4</span></span>
<span id="cb81-20"><a href="#cb81-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb81-21"><a href="#cb81-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">foo</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb81-22"><a href="#cb81-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="dv">2</span>)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb81-23"><a href="#cb81-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="cf">await</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">resolve</span>(<span class="dv">8</span>))<span class="op">;</span></span>

<span id="cb82-110"><a href="#cb82-110" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">/**</span></span>
<span id="cb82-111"><a href="#cb82-111" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * Promise.then()返回的promise的结果由什么所决定？</span></span>
<span id="cb82-112"><a href="#cb82-112" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （1）简单表达：由then() 指定的回调函数 执行的结果 决定</span></span>
<span id="cb82-113"><a href="#cb82-113" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （2）详细表达：</span></span>
<span id="cb82-114"><a href="#cb82-114" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> *      ①如果抛出异常，新promise变为reject,reason为抛出的异常。</span></span>
<span id="cb82-115"><a href="#cb82-115" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> *      ②如果返回的是非promise的值，新promise变为resolved,value为返回的值</span></span>
<span id="cb82-116"><a href="#cb82-116" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> *      ③如果返回的是另一个新的promise,次promise的结果就会编程新promise的结果</span></span>
<span id="cb82-117"><a href="#cb82-117" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> */</span></span>
<span id="cb82-118"><a href="#cb82-118" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span> reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb82-119"><a href="#cb82-119" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>     <span class="fu">resolve</span>(<span class="dv">1</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//onResolved1() 1 onResolved2() undefined</span></span>
<span id="cb82-120"><a href="#cb82-120" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="co">//  reject(1);//onRejected1() 1 onResolved2() undefined</span></span>
<span id="cb82-121"><a href="#cb82-121" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(</span>
<span id="cb82-122"><a href="#cb82-122" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    value <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb82-123"><a href="#cb82-123" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;onResolved1()&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>value)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb82-124"><a href="#cb82-124" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="dv">2</span></span>
<span id="cb82-125"><a href="#cb82-125" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co">// return Promise.resolve(3)</span></span>
<span id="cb82-126"><a href="#cb82-126" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co">// return Promise.reject(4)</span></span>
<span id="cb82-127"><a href="#cb82-127" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="co">// throw 5</span></span>
<span id="cb82-128"><a href="#cb82-128" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb82-129"><a href="#cb82-129" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    reason <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb82-130"><a href="#cb82-130" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;onRejected1()&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>reason)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb82-131"><a href="#cb82-131" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb82-132"><a href="#cb82-132" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(</span>
<span id="cb82-133"><a href="#cb82-133" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    value <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb82-134"><a href="#cb82-134" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;onResolved2()&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>value)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb82-135"><a href="#cb82-135" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }<span class="op">,</span></span>
<span id="cb82-136"><a href="#cb82-136" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    reason <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb82-137"><a href="#cb82-137" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;onRejected2()&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>reason)<span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb82-138"><a href="#cb82-138" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb82-139"><a href="#cb82-139" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>)</span>
<span id="cb82-140"><a href="#cb82-140" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a></span>
<span id="cb82-141"><a href="#cb82-141" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">/**</span></span>
<span id="cb82-142"><a href="#cb82-142" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * Promise如何串联多个操作任务？</span></span>
<span id="cb82-143"><a href="#cb82-143" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （1）promise的then()返回的一个新的promise,可以开成then()的链式调用。</span></span>
<span id="cb82-144"><a href="#cb82-144" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * （2）通过then的链式调用串连多个同步/异步任务</span></span>

<span id="cb82-146"><a href="#cb82-146" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span> ((resolve<span class="op">,</span> reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb82-147"><a href="#cb82-147" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(() <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>

<span id="cb82-164"><a href="#cb82-164" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * promise异常穿透？</span></span>
<span id="cb82-165"><a href="#cb82-165" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * (1)当使用promise的then链式调用时，可以在最后 指定失败的回调。</span></span>
<span id="cb82-166"><a href="#cb82-166" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * (2)前面任何操作做出了异常，都会传到最后失败的回调处理。</span></span>
<span id="cb82-167"><a href="#cb82-167" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * 中断promise链？</span></span>
<span id="cb82-168"><a href="#cb82-168" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * (1)当使用promise的then链式调用时，在中间中断，不再调用后面的回调函数</span></span>
<span id="cb82-169"><a href="#cb82-169" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> * (2)办法：在回调函数中返回一个pending状态的promise对象</span></span>
<span id="cb82-170"><a href="#cb82-170" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co"> */</span></span>
<span id="cb82-171"><a href="#cb82-171" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span> ((resolve<span class="op">,</span> reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb82-172"><a href="#cb82-172" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    <span class="fu">resolve</span>(<span class="dv">1</span>)</span>

<span id="cb82-176"><a href="#cb82-176" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>

<p><strong>宏任务跟微任务</strong>：</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb83"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb83-1"><a href="#cb83-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>      <span class="co">/**</span></span>
<span id="cb83-2"><a href="#cb83-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         * 1.JS中用来存储执行回调函数的队列包含2个不同特定的队列</span></span>
<span id="cb83-3"><a href="#cb83-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         * 2.宏队列：用来保存待执行的宏任务（回调），比如：dom事件回调、Ajax回调、定时器setTime回调</span></span>
<span id="cb83-4"><a href="#cb83-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         * 3.微嘟列：用来保存待执行的微任务（回调），比如：promise回调、MutaionOberver回调</span></span>

<p><strong>async 函数和await 函数</strong></p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb84"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb84-1"><a href="#cb84-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>          <span class="co">/**</span></span>
<span id="cb84-2"><a href="#cb84-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         * 1.async 函数</span></span>
<span id="cb84-3"><a href="#cb84-3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         *   函数的返回值为promise对象。</span></span>
<span id="cb84-4"><a href="#cb84-4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         *   promise对象的结果由async函数执行的返回值决定。</span></span>
<span id="cb84-5"><a href="#cb84-5" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         * 2.await 表达式</span></span>
<span id="cb84-6"><a href="#cb84-6" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         *   await 右侧的表达式一般为promise对象，但也可以是其他的值，</span></span>
<span id="cb84-7"><a href="#cb84-7" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         *   如果表达式是promsie对象，await返回的是promise成功的值，</span></span>
<span id="cb84-8"><a href="#cb84-8" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         *   如果表达式是其他值，直接将此值作为await的返回值。</span></span>
<span id="cb84-9"><a href="#cb84-9" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         *   </span></span>
<span id="cb84-10"><a href="#cb84-10" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="co">         */</span></span>
<span id="cb84-11"><a href="#cb84-11" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">fn1</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb84-12"><a href="#cb84-12" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="dv">1</span></span>
<span id="cb84-13"><a href="#cb84-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="co">// throw 2</span></span>
<span id="cb84-14"><a href="#cb84-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="co">// return Promise.reject(3)</span></span>
<span id="cb84-15"><a href="#cb84-15" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        }</span>
<span id="cb84-16"><a href="#cb84-16" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="kw">const</span> result <span class="op">=</span> <span class="fu">fn1</span>()</span>
<span id="cb84-17"><a href="#cb84-17" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        result<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">then</span>(</span>
<span id="cb84-18"><a href="#cb84-18" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            value <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb84-19"><a href="#cb84-19" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;onResolved&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>value)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//onResolved 1</span></span>
<span id="cb84-20"><a href="#cb84-20" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            }<span class="op">,</span>reason <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb84-21"><a href="#cb84-21" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                <span class="bu">console</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">log</span>(<span class="st">&#39;onRejected&#39;</span><span class="op">,</span>reason)</span>
<span id="cb84-22"><a href="#cb84-22" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            }</span>
<span id="cb84-23"><a href="#cb84-23" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        )</span>
<span id="cb84-24"><a href="#cb84-24" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        <span class="kw">function</span> <span class="fu">fn2</span>(){</span>
<span id="cb84-25"><a href="#cb84-25" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            <span class="cf">return</span> <span class="kw">new</span> <span class="bu">Promise</span>((resolve<span class="op">,</span> reject) <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb84-26"><a href="#cb84-26" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                <span class="pp">setTimeout</span>(() <span class="kw">=&gt;</span> {</span>
<span id="cb84-27"><a href="#cb84-27" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>                    <span class="fu">reject</span>(<span class="dv">6</span>)</span>

<span id="cb84-29"><a href="#cb84-29" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>            })</span>
<span id="cb84-30"><a href="#cb84-30" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>        }</span>

<hr />
<h3 id="第12章bom">第12章——BOM</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>12.1 Windwos对象</strong></li>
</ul>
<p>BOM
的核心是windows对象，windows对象有两个身份，另一个是ECMAScript中的Global对象，另一个是浏览器窗口的JavaScript接口。</p>
<p><strong>BOM和DOM的区别:</strong></p>
<p>①
DOM：文档对象模型，描述了处理网页内容的方法和接口(windows.document)。</p>
<p>②
BOM：浏览器对象模型，描述了与浏览器进行交互的方法和接口(navigater、history、screen、location、windows)。</p>
<hr />
<h3 id="第13章客户端检测">第13章——客户端检测</h3>
<ul>
<li>能力检测：检测浏览器是否含有某种特性</li>
<li>用户代理检测：通过用户代理字符串确定浏览器。</li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h3 id="第14章dom">第14章——DOM</h3>
<p>DOM表示由多层节点构成的文档，DOM树。</p>
<p>Element Traversal API 五个属性：</p>
<p>childElementCount，返回元素数量（不包含文本节点和注释）。</p>
<p>firstElementChild，指向第一个Element类型的子元素。</p>
<p>lastElementChild，指向最后一个Element类型的子元素。</p>
<p>previousElementSibling,指向前一个Element类型的同胞元素。</p>
<p>nextElementSibling,指向后一个Element类型的同胞元素。</p>
<hr />
<h3 id="第15章dom拓展">第15章——DOM拓展</h3>
<ul>
<li><p><strong>15.1 Selectors API</strong></p></li>
<li><p>querySelector()返回匹配该模式的第一个后代元素，如果没有匹配项则返回结果null。</p>

<hr />
<h3 id="第17章事件">第17章——事件</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>17.1 事件流：页面接收事件的顺序。</strong></li>
<li>事件传播的三个阶段：</li>
<li>①事件捕获阶段：事件是从Document节点自上而下向目标节点传播。</li>
<li>②目标阶段：达到事件对象的事件目标，找到目标节点后完成后停止。</li>
<li>③事件冒泡阶段：事件再从目标节点自下而上向Document节点传播。 <img
src="https://p3-juejin.byteimg.com/tos-cn-i-k3u1fbpfcp/842e8c29f9d0410a9a1690f530938cb9~tplv-k3u1fbpfcp-zoom-in-crop-mark:1512:0:0:0.awebp"
loading="lazy" alt="在这里插入图片描述" /></li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h3 id="第20章streams-api">第20章——Streams API</h3>
<ul>
<li><p>20.2
跨上下文消息：一种执行在不同上下文间传递消息的能力。核心是postMessage()方法。</p></li>
<li><p>postMessage()方法接收三个参数：消息（data）、文档源（origin）、文档中的windows对象代理（souce）。</p></li>
<li><div class="sourceCode" id="cb86"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb86-1"><a href="#cb86-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">let</span> iframeWindow <span class="op">=</span> <span class="bu">document</span><span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">getElementById</span>(<span class="st">&quot;myframe&quot;</span>)<span class="op">.</span><span class="at">contentWindow</span><span class="op">;</span></span>
<span id="cb86-2"><a href="#cb86-2" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>iframeWindow<span class="op">.</span><span class="fu">postMessage</span>(<span class="st">&quot;A secret&quot;</span><span class="op">,</span><span class="st">&quot;http://www.xxxx.com&quot;</span>)<span class="op">;</span><span class="co">//指定源www.xxx.com,x`向内嵌窗格发送一条消息</span></span></code></pre></div></li>
<li><p>Streams API</p></li>
<li><p>可读流：通过公共接口读取数据块的流，由<strong>消费者</strong>进行处理，使用getReader()方法获取流的锁</p>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb87"><pre
class="sourceCode javascript"><code class="sourceCode javascript"><span id="cb87-1"><a href="#cb87-1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a><span class="kw">async</span> <span class="kw">function</span><span class="op">*</span> <span class="fu">ints</span>(){</span>

<span id="cb87-13"><a href="#cb87-13" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>    }</span>
<span id="cb87-14"><a href="#cb87-14" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1"></a>})</span></code></pre></div></li>
<li><p>可写流：通过公共接口写入数据块的流，<strong>生产者</strong>将数据写入流。</p></li>
<li><p>转换流：包含可读流和可写流，可根据需要检查和修改流内容。</p></li>
<li><p>20.11 Web组件</p></li>
<li><p>一套用于增强DOM行为的工具，包括影子DOM、自定义元素和HTML模板。</p></li>
<li><p>影子DOM通过attachShadow()方法创建并添加给有效HTML元素。</p></li>
</ul>
<div class="sourceCode" id="cb88"><pre

<hr />
<h3 id="第23章解析与序列化">第23章——解析与序列化</h3>
<ul>
<li>23.2 JSON对象</li>
<li>序列化：stringify()方法，第一个<strong>参数</strong>是过滤器，可以是数组或函数；第二个<strong>参数</strong>用于缩进结果JSON字符串的选项。</li>
<li>解析：parse()方法又叫复活函数，包含两个参数，属性名（key）和属性值（value）。可以接收一个额外的参数，这个函数会正对每个键/值对都调用一次。</li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h3 id="第24章网络请求与远程资源">第24章——网络请求与远程资源</h3>
<ul>
<li>GET请求：用于向服务器查询某些信息。</li>
<li>POSE请求：哟用于向服务器发送应该保存的信息。</li>
<li>Fetch API ：浏览器会向给定的URL发送请求，读取响应、处理状态码</li>
<li>Web
Socket（套接字）：通过一个<strong>长时连接</strong>实现与<strong>服务器</strong>全双工、双向的通信。在JavaScript创建Web
Socket的时候，一个HTTP请求会发送到服务器以初始化连接，服务器响应后，连接使用的Upgrade头部从HTTP切换到Web
Socket协议，使用该协议的专有服务器。</li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h3 id="第26章模块">第26章——模块</h3>
<ul>
<li>本质上是键/值实体，</li>
<li>ES6模块默认在严格模式下执行，不共享全局命名空间。</li>
</ul>
<hr />
<h3 id="第27章工作者线程">第27章——工作者线程</h3>
<ul>
<li>JavaScript是单线程的，为了为了解决并发问题，JavaScript提出了工作者线程的三种类型</li>
<li>专用工作者线程：让脚本单独创建一个JavaScript线程，以执行委托的任务。</li>
<li>共享工作者线程：创建到的线程可以别多个不同的上下文使用，包括不同的页面。</li>
<li>服务工作者线程：拦截、重定向和修改页面发出的请求，充当王阔请求仲裁者的角色。</li>
</ul>
